     <!-- -->
     <span class="break-words tvm-parent-container">
      <!-- -->
      <span>
       <span class="text-view-model" dir="ltr">
        Job Title: Sr. Golang Backend Developer
        <br/>
        Location: Hybrid from Cincinnati/Blue Ash, OH
        <br/>
        Job Type: Contract
        <br/>
        Client preference visa independent candidates only
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Skills/Experience:
        <br/>
        Microservices (MUST-HAVE!!!!)
        <br/>
        Experience working with high-volume applications.
        <br/>
        Both GO and Java experience (Experience with both is not a requirement but this would be a differentiator)
        <br/>
        Note: Candidates must be able to collaborate with offshore teams.
        <br/>
        Project: Backend development on a customer platform/profile. Will also provide production support.
        <br/>
        Specific skillsets we are looking for (in addition to the developer requirements we expect):
        <br/>
        * Senior Backend services developer
        <br/>
        * Experience with high throughput, distributed multi-region applications and databases
        <br/>
        * Backend REST micro services development experience
        <br/>
        * Deploying and maintaining micro services to Kubernetes
        <br/>
        * Expertise in Go language and/or Java (preferably Go)
        <br/>
        * Cloud expertise (preferably Azure)
        <br/>
        * Experience with distributed SQL and NOSQL databases
        <br/>
        * Expertise with CI/CD workflows (preferably Github)
        <br/>
        * Ability to work with remote offshore teams
        <br/>
        Key Responsibilities
        <br/>
        • Lead and participate in the design and implementation of large and/or architecturally significant applications.
        <br/>
        • Champion company standards and best practices. Work to continuously improve software delivery processes and practices.
        <br/>
        • Build partnerships across the application, business and infrastructure teams.
        <br/>
        • Develop programming specifications. Design, code and unit test application code using Software Development Life Cycle (SDLC) best practices.
        <br/>
        • Complete estimates and work plans independently as appropriate for design, development, implementation and rollout tasks.
        <br/>
        • Create technical system documentation and ensure that this documentation remains current throughout all phases of the SDLC.
        <br/>
        • Participate in all phases of system testing.
        <br/>
        • Communicate with the appropriate teams to ensure that assignments are managed appropriately and that completed assignments are of the highest quality.
        <br/>
        If you are interested, please send me your updated resume at
        <a data-attribute-index="0" href="mailto:Labrez.k@kksoftwareassociates.com" target="_self">
         Labrez.k@kksoftwareassociates.com
        </a>
        . Thank you so much.

       <span class="text-view-model" dir="ltr">
        Title - Software Developer - Microservices
        <br/>
        Duration - Contract to hire
        <br/>
        Location - Cincinnati, OH (Hybrid - M/T/W (3days onsite))
        <br/>
        Looking for GC and USC only.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Headcount: 2
        <br/>
        Previous prescreen scores within 45 days will transfer in. 5 questions, a game and a coding challenge
        <br/>
        Interview: First round: 30-minute screening with Tech lead/HM. Second Round: Panel interview with technical screening.
        <br/>
        Must be local to Cincinnati. No office day requirements currently but that could change in the future, please advise candidates of this.
        <br/>
        NOTE: Please do not submit any candidates that were submitted to Job #10353, they will be automatically rejected and not reviewed. Experience with Microservices is a MUST for all submissions.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Standout Skills/Experience:
        <br/>
        ·        Microservices (MUST-HAVE!!!!)
        <br/>
        ·        Experience working with high-volume applications
        <br/>
        ·        Both GO and Java experience (Experience with both is not a requirement but this would be a differentiator)
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Note: Candidates must be able to collaborate with offshore teams.
        <br/>
        Project: Backend development on a customer platform/profile. Will also provide production support.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Typical Duties
        <br/>
        ·        Lead and participate in designing and implementing large and/or architecturally significant applications.
        <br/>
        ·        Champion company standards and best practices, continuously improving software delivery processes.
        <br/>
        ·        Foster partnerships across application, business, and infrastructure teams.
        <br/>
        ·        Develop programming specifications and code, adhering to SDLC best practices.
        <br/>
        ·        Independently complete estimates and work plans for design, development, and implementation tasks.
        <br/>
        ·        Create and maintain technical system documentation throughout the SDLC phases.
        <br/>
        ·        Participate in all system testing phases.
        <br/>
        ·        Communicate effectively with relevant teams to ensure proper assignment management and high-quality deliverables.
        <br/>
        Requirements
        <br/>
        ·        Experience in developing high throughput, distributed multi-region applications and databases
        <br/>
        ·        Proficiency in backend REST microservices development
        <br/>
        ·        Deployment and maintenance of microservices to Kubernetes
        <br/>
        ·        Expertise in Go language and/or Java, preferably Go
        <br/>
        ·        Cloud proficiency, preferably in Azure
        <br/>
        ·        Experience with distributed SQL and NoSQL databases
        <br/>
        ·        Proficiency with CI/CD workflows, preferably in Github
        <br/>
        ·        Ability to collaborate effectively with remote offshore teams
        <br/>
        Please share resume to
        <a data-attribute-index="0" href="mailto:rick@sun-itsolutions.com" target="_self">
         rick@sun-itsolutions.com
        </a>

      <span>
       <span class="text-view-model" dir="ltr">
        Position : Sr. Golang Developer
        <br/>
        Location: Cincinnati/Blue Ash, OH ,
        <br/>
        Job Type: C2C (12 Month Contract + (Possible extension)
        <br/>
        <br/>
        <br/>
        RESPONSIBILITIES
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Client –Kroger
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Must have a Linkedin profile.
        <br/>
        Visa Status : OPEN
        <br/>
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Skills/Experience:
        <br/>
        Microservices (MUST-HAVE!!!!)
        <br/>
        Experience working with high-volume applications.
        <br/>
        Both GO and Java experience (Experience with both is not a requirement but this would be a differentiator)
        <br/>
        Note: Candidates must be able to collaborate with offshore teams.
        <br/>
        Project: Backend development on a customer platform/profile. Will also provide production support.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Job Description
        <br/>
        The Developer is responsible for leading the design, development, testing, debugging, maintaining and documenting software components to which they are assigned. The Developer will be involved in the technical design process and completes estimates and work plans for design, development, implementation, and rollout tasks. The Developer also communicates with the appropriate teams to ensure that assignments are delivered with the highest of quality and in accordance to standards. The Developer strives to continuously improve the software delivery processes and practices.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Specific skillsets we are looking for (in addition to the developer requirements we expect):
        <br/>
        * Senior Backend services developer
        <br/>
        * Experience with high throughput, distributed multi-region applications and databases
        <br/>
        * Backend REST micro services development experience
        <br/>
        * Deploying and maintaining micro services to Kubernetes
        <br/>
        * Expertise in Go language and/or Java (preferably Go)
        <br/>
        * Cloud expertise (preferably Azure)
        <br/>
        * Experience with distributed SQL and NOSQL databases
        <br/>
        * Expertise with CI/CD workflows (preferably Github)
        <br/>
        * Ability to work with remote offshore teams
        <br/>
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Key Responsibilities
        <br/>
        • Lead and participate in the design and implementation of large and/or architecturally significant applications.
        <br/>
        • Champion company standards and best practices. Work to continuously improve software delivery processes and practices.
        <br/>
        • Build partnerships across the application, business and infrastructure teams.
        <br/>
        • Develop programming specifications. Design, code and unit test application code using Software Development Life Cycle (SDLC) best practices.
        <br/>
        • Complete estimates and work plans independently as appropriate for design, development, implementation and rollout tasks.
        <br/>
        • Create technical system documentation and ensure that this documentation remains current throughout all phases of the SDLC.
        <br/>
        • Participate in all phases of system testing.
        <br/>
        • Communicate with the appropriate teams to ensure that assignments are managed appropriately and that completed assignments are of the highest quality
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Email :
        <a data-attribute-index="0" href="mailto:naresh@equitasitinc.com" target="_self">
         naresh@equitasitinc.com
        </a>
       </span>

  <div class="feed-shared-update-v2__description-wrapper mr2" style="" tabindex="-1">
   <div class="feed-shared-inline-show-more-text feed-shared-update-v2__description feed-shared-inline-show-more-text--minimal-padding feed-shared-inline-show-more-text--3-lines" tabindex="-1">
    <div class="update-components-text relative update-components-update-v2__commentary" dir="ltr">
     <!-- -->
     <span class="break-words tvm-parent-container">
      <!-- -->
      <span>
       <span class="text-view-model" dir="ltr">
        We are looking for a Project Manager for our US based clients to join our team.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        A Project Manager of project management experience that can help us achieving the following for our US based clients :
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Responsible for ensuring consistent reporting, risk mitigation, time line, and cost control.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        To help ensure that the software development process works as it is intended.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        To work closely with the Functional Managers in order to facilitate, encourage, and prioritize the process.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Plan, execute, monitor, control, and close projects based on Project Management best practices.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Setup required communications and meetings with offshore clients to collect requirements, prepare scope.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Produce project deliverables on time, within budget and within scope and maintain an updated Project Schedule at all times.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Professional development and training for team members.
        <br/>
        Responsible for preparing and reporting status reports to higher management.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Make sure that the process goes forward and use a variety of processes, meetings, and documents (artifacts) to ensure continued forward progress and to identify problems as soon as possible.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Make sure everybody follow guidelines and processes define by the company and monitor them.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Make certain that the development team keeps versions and configurations in proper version control.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Must make sure that lessons learned are shared with the required personnel.
        <br/>
        Responsible of the on-time delivery of the solution.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Must abide by all company policies and procedures.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Education:

       <span class="text-view-model" dir="ltr">
        Warm Greetings...! From Evoke Technologies (
        <a data-attribute-index="0" href="http://www.evoketechnologies.com" target="_self">
         www.evoketechnologies.com
        </a>
        )
        <br/>
        Little brief about us: Evoke Technologies is a leading global IT services consulting company. Incorporated in 2003, Evoke has developed a proven roadmap for offshore outsourcing, software development, maintenance and support that delivers, We boost our partners’ business, using the most advanced technology and the best professionals in the sector.
        <br/>
        Evoke has more than 1300 employees across our offices in USA, India, Poland (Wroclaw), Australia, and UK
        <br/>
        We are Looking for an Automation Test Engineer Position.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        The Role:
        <br/>
        <br/>
        We are looking for a Software Test Engineer to join our Testing Team. We are looking for a talented, self-driven and customer focused Automation Test Engineer, someone who is passionate about writing and maintaining high-quality software that solves real-world meaningful problems at scale. This is an exciting opportunity for highly motivated individuals to work in a fast-paced customer focused Role.
        <br/>
        As part of an agile development team, you will play a key role in defining and shaping new products and systems to deliver a better experience for our client projects.
        <br/>
        Location: Wroclaw – Poland.
        <br/>
        Mode of Work – Hybrid
        <br/>
        <br/>
        The JD is as follows:
        <br/>
        Minimum 3+ Years exp in Manual Teasting
        <br/>
        Selenium WebDriver with 1+years exp.,
        <br/>
        Experience in Xpath and CSS Selector is added advantage.
        <br/>
        Should work independently and coordinate with the client teams.
        <br/>
        Strong customer focus, problem solving and analytical ability.
        <br/>
        Knowledge on TFS.
        <br/>
        Excellent Communication.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Send your CV to
        <a data-attribute-index="1" href="mailto:msarana@evoketechnologies.com" target="_self">
         msarana@evoketechnologies.com
        </a>
        and join our team!

        <br/>
        Must be local to Cincinnati. No office day requirements currently but that could change in the future, please advise candidates of this.
        <br/>
        NOTE: Please do not submit any candidates that were submitted to Job #10353, they will be automatically rejected and not reviewed. Experience with Microservices is a MUST for all submissions.

        <br/>
        ·        Microservices (MUST-HAVE!!!!)
        <br/>
        ·        Experience working with high-volume applications
        <br/>
        ·        Both GO and Java experience (Experience with both is not a requirement but this would be a differentiator)
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Note: Candidates must be able to collaborate with offshore teams.
        <br/>
        Project: Backend development on a customer platform/profile. Will also provide production support.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Typical Duties
        <br/>
        ·        Lead and participate in designing and implementing large and/or architecturally significant applications.
        <br/>
        ·        Champion company standards and best practices, continuously improving software delivery processes.
        <br/>

        <br/>
        ·        Create and maintain technical system documentation throughout the SDLC phases.
        <br/>
        ·        Participate in all system testing phases.
        <br/>
        ·        Communicate effectively with relevant teams to ensure proper assignment management and high-quality deliverables.
        <br/>

        <br/>
        ·        Experience in developing high throughput, distributed multi-region applications and databases
        <br/>
        ·        Proficiency in backend REST microservices development
        <br/>
        ·        Deployment and maintenance of microservices to Kubernetes
        <br/>
        ·        Expertise in Go language and/or Java, preferably Go
        <br/>

        <br/>

        <br/>

        <br/>

        <br/>

        <br/>

        <br/>

        <br/>

        <br/>

        <br/>
        - Experience writing unit and functional tests

        <br/>

        <br/>

        <br/>

        <br/>
        - Experience with database technologies and data modeling.
        <br/>

        <br/>

        <br/>

        Most Urgent for NCR Delhi-Noida
        <br/>
        Full Stack JAVA Web Development Architect -3-5 nos
        <br/>
        Exp. 10-15yrs
        <br/>
        Location: Noida, Work from office
        <br/>
        *AWS SCALA,JAVA,Spring boot,ReactJS/Angular
        <br/>
        <br/>
        We are looking Full Stack JAVA Web Development Architect for Telecom SW app. Development co. of USA.. and Group Turnover which is 160B$ co.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Job Description
        <br/>
        We are looking for Full Stack JAVA Web Development Architect to work with our high-caliber group in delivering complex multi-platform applications for the next generation of telecommunications and fraud protection.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Core Requirements:
        <br/>
        - 10 or more years of extensive full-stack experience and application design patterns
        <br/>
        - At least 5 years of hands on experience with React, or Angular, Spring Boot
        <br/>
        - At least 5 years experience using Java and Scala
        <br/>
        - At least 5 years experience designing and building RESTful services.
        <br/>
        - Strong experience developing web applications and understanding of new web technologies
        <br/>
        - Strong experience using AUTH technologies such as OAuth2, LDAP/SAML a plus
        <br/>
        - Experience building highly-available applications
        <br/>
        - Experience building/hosting production applications on AWS or any other major cloud provider
        <br/>
        - Experience writing SQL queries
        <br/>
        - Basic understanding of networking concepts
        <br/>
        - Working knowledge of web service infrastructure such as DNS, load balancers, reverse proxies, CDNs, application Servers, and databases
        <br/>
        - Strong experience with Git
        <br/>
        - Experience setting up CI/CD for new applications and development workflows
        <br/>
        - Experience writing unit and functional tests
        <br/>
        Preferred Qualifications:
        <br/>
        - Exposure to AI / ML based applications.
        <br/>
        - Experience working in a product development company focused on Telecommunications
        <br/>
        - Proficient with edge computing principals and architecture.
        <br/>
        - Experience with Agile scrum methodologies.
        <br/>
        - Experience with database technologies and data modeling.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Responsibilities:
        <br/>
        Responsible for the architecture of new products and enhancements – Concepts, Architecture, Design &amp; work with teams for delivery, roll-out, and Customer Success.
        <br/>
        Architect scalable, robust, and cost-effective solutions in a public and hybrid cloud environment.
        <br/>
        Establish a common set of architecture and design principles that the various engineering groups should adhere to.
        <br/>
        Actively research industry-wide frameworks and integrate them into the platform needs.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        About Co.
        <br/>
        Our customer working in Telecom ,Retail ,Engineering and Fintech
        <a data-attribute-index="0" href="http://domain.as" target="_self">
         domain.as
        </a>
        Software Application Development Product co. HQ is in Virginia USA and offshore Devp. Center in India in Noida .
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Pl share the cv those have relevant exp. and ready to work Noida location.

      <span>
       <span class="text-view-model" dir="ltr">
        About the job
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Company Overview
        <br/>
        <br/>
        10Pearls is an end-to-end digital technology services partner helping businesses utilize technology as a competitive advantage. We help our customers digitalize their existing business, build innovative new products, and augment their existing teams with high performance team members. Our broad expertise in product management, user experience/design, cloud architecture, software development, data insights and intelligence, cyber security, emerging tech, and quality assurance ensures that we are delivering solutions that address business needs. 10Pearls is proud to have a diverse clientele including large enterprises, SMBs and high growth startups. We work with clients across industries, including healthcare/life sciences, education, energy, communications/media, financial services, and hi-tech. Our many long-term, successful partnerships are built upon trust, integrity and successful delivery and execution.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Role
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Looking to add a Finance Executive to our team. The ideal candidate should have 2-4 years of relevant experience and good knowledge of accounting and bookkeeping procedures
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Responsibilities
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Maintenance of proper books of accounts
        <br/>
        Timely and accurate preparation of bank and credit card reconciliations
        <br/>
        Management of Receivable &amp; Payable functions
        <br/>
        Ensuring timely payments and adequate recording in Sage Intacct
        <br/>
        Invoicing to clients and follow up of outstanding accounts receivable
        <br/>
        Execution of core financial processes including customer / vendor setup, administration of bank accounts, and customer / vendor reconciliation
        <br/>
        Preparation of monthly management accounts
        <br/>
        Liaising with offshore accounting teams regarding day-to-day financial operations
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Requirements
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Graduation from reputed university or ACCA / ICMA qualified
        <br/>
        Good knowledge of accounting and bookkeeping procedures
        <br/>
        Advanced MS Excel skills
        <br/>
        Excellent communication &amp; social skills
        <br/>
        Strong attention to detail
        <br/>
        <a data-attribute-index="0" href="https://lnkd.in/d_QxEuTu" target="_self">
         https://lnkd.in/d_QxEuTu
        </a>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>

        Most Urgent for NCR Delhi-Noida
        <br/>
        Full Stack JAVA Web Development Architect -3-5 nos
        <br/>
        Exp. 10-15yrs
        <br/>
        Location: Noida, Work from office
        <br/>

        <br/>
        <br/>
        We are looking Full Stack JAVA Web Development Architect for Telecom SW app. Development co. of USA.. and Group Turnover which is 160B$ co.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Job Description
        <br/>
        We are looking for Full Stack JAVA Web Development Architect to work with our high-caliber group in delivering complex multi-platform applications for the next generation of telecommunications and fraud protection.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Core Requirements:
        <br/>
        - 10 or more years of extensive full-stack experience and application design patterns
        <br/>
        - At least 5 years of hands on experience with React, or Angular, Spring Boot
        <br/>
        - At least 5 years experience using Java and Scala
        <br/>
        - At least 5 years experience designing and building RESTful services.
        <br/>
        - Strong experience developing web applications and understanding of new web technologies
        <br/>
        - Strong experience using AUTH technologies such as OAuth2, LDAP/SAML a plus
        <br/>
        - Experience building highly-available applications
        <br/>
        - Experience building/hosting production applications on AWS or any other major cloud provider
        <br/>
        - Experience writing SQL queries
        <br/>
        - Basic understanding of networking concepts
        <br/>
        - Working knowledge of web service infrastructure such as DNS, load balancers, reverse proxies, CDNs, application Servers, and databases
        <br/>
        - Strong experience with Git
        <br/>
        - Experience setting up CI/CD for new applications and development workflows
        <br/>
        - Experience writing unit and functional tests
        <br/>
        Preferred Qualifications:
        <br/>
        - Exposure to AI / ML based applications.
        <br/>
        - Experience working in a product development company focused on Telecommunications
        <br/>
        - Proficient with edge computing principals and architecture.
        <br/>
        - Experience with Agile scrum methodologies.
        <br/>
        - Experience with database technologies and data modeling.
        <br/>
        <br/>
        Responsibilities:
        <br/>
        Responsible for the architecture of new products and enhancements – Concepts, Architecture, Design &amp; work with teams for delivery, roll-out, and Customer Success.
        <br/>
        Architect scalable, robust, and cost-effective solutions in a public and hybrid cloud environment.
        <br/>
        Establish a common set of architecture and design principles that the various engineering groups should adhere to.
        <br/>
        Actively research industry-wide frameworks and integrate them into the platform needs.
